  INTRODUCTION:

All praise be to God, the Lord of all creation, and may peace and blessings be upon the Trustworthy Messenger, his family, his companions and all those who follow him:

The clash between the evidence pointing out to its prohibition and the evidence that points to its permissibility, reached the point where those who argued for it being forbidden claimed the occurence of abrogation, others maintained that there was a restriction, and another group went to provide different interpretations of the verses.   CONCLUSION:

To conclude, the present researcher has made a critical study of the á¸¥adÄ«th of Suhayl â€œdonâ€™t initiate the greeting of peace (al-SalÄm) with polytheistsâ€, whom there is some disagreement on: among the leading scholars who considered him to be reliable (thiqa) are Aá¸¥mad and Muslim who included some of his narrations and was criticized for thatâ€”as mentioned by al-á¸¤Äkim.
